BUG: Variable not defined when awaited and rendered inside a snippet
### Describe the bug

I’m using the experimental `async` flag.

When rendering an awaited variable inside a snippet — without explicitly declaring it in the snippet parameters — the console throws the following error:

```
Uncaught (in promise) ReferenceError: value is not defined
```

I’m currently on **v5.38.3**. This was working correctly in **v5.38.2**.

/** @import { AssignmentPattern, BlockStatement, Expression, Identifier, Statement } from 'estree' */
/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../types' */
import { dev } from '../../../../state.js';
import { extract_paths } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
import { get_value } from './shared/declarations.js';

/**
 * @param {AST.SnippetBlock} node
 * @param {ComponentContext} context
 */
export function SnippetBlock(node, context) {
	// TODO hoist where possible
	/** @type {(Identifier | AssignmentPattern)[]} */
	const args = [b.id('$$anchor')];
	const has_await = node.body.metadata.has_await || false;

	/** @type {BlockStatement} */
	let body;

	/** @type {Statement[]} */
	const declarations = [];

	const transform = { ...context.state.transform };
	const child_state = { ...context.state, transform };

	for (let i = 0; i < node.parameters.length; i++) {
		const argument = node.parameters[i];

		if (!argument) continue;

		if (argument.type === 'Identifier') {
			args.push(b.assignment_pattern(argument, b.id('$.noop')));
			transform[argument.name] = { read: b.call };

			continue;
		}

		let arg_alias = `$$arg${i}`;
		args.push(b.id(arg_alias));

		const { inserts, paths } = extract_paths(argument, b.maybe_call(b.id(arg_alias)));

		for (const { id, value } of inserts) {
			id.name = context.state.scope.generate('$$array');
			transform[id.name] = { read: get_value };

			declarations.push(
				b.var(id, b.call('$.derived', /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(b.thunk(value)))))
			);
		}

		for (const path of paths) {
			const name = /** @type {Identifier} */ (path.node).name;
			const needs_derived = path.has_default_value; // to ensure that default value is only called once
			const fn = b.thunk(/** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(path.expression, child_state)));

			declarations.push(b.let(path.node, needs_derived ? b.call('$.derived_safe_equal', fn) : fn));

			transform[name] = {
				read: needs_derived ? get_value : b.call
			};

			// we need to eagerly evaluate the expression in order to hit any
			// 'Cannot access x before initialization' errors
			if (dev) {
				declarations.push(b.stmt(transform[name].read(b.id(name))));
			}
		}
	}
	const block = /** @type {BlockStatement} */ (context.visit(node.body, child_state)).body;
	body = b.block([
		dev ? b.stmt(b.call('$.validate_snippet_args', b.spread(b.id('arguments')))) : b.empty,
		...declarations,
		...block
	]);

	// in dev we use a FunctionExpression (not arrow function) so we can use `arguments`
	let snippet = dev
		? b.call(
				'$.wrap_snippet',
				b.id(context.state.analysis.name),
				b.function(null, args, body, has_await)
			)
		: b.arrow(args, body, has_await);

	const declaration = b.const(node.expression, snippet);

	// Top-level snippets are hoisted so they can be referenced in the `<script>`
	if (context.path.length === 1 && context.path[0].type === 'Fragment') {
		if (node.metadata.can_hoist) {
			context.state.module_level_snippets.push(declaration);
		} else {
			context.state.instance_level_snippets.push(declaration);
		}
	} else {
		context.state.init.push(declaration);
	}
}

/** @import { BlockStatement, Pattern, Statement } from 'estree' */
/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
/** @import { ComponentClientTransformState, ComponentContext } from '../types' */
import { extract_identifiers, is_expression_async } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
import { create_derived } from '../utils.js';
import { get_value } from './shared/declarations.js';
import { build_expression, add_svelte_meta } from './shared/utils.js';

/**
 * @param {AST.AwaitBlock} node
 * @param {ComponentContext} context
 */
export function AwaitBlock(node, context) {
	context.state.template.push_comment();

	// Visit {#await <expression>} first to ensure that scopes are in the correct order
	const expression = b.thunk(
		build_expression(context, node.expression, node.metadata.expression),
		node.metadata.expression.has_await
	);

	let then_block;
	let catch_block;

	if (node.then) {
		const then_context = {
			...context,
			state: { ...context.state, transform: { ...context.state.transform } }
		};
		const argument = node.value && create_derived_block_argument(node.value, then_context);

		/** @type {Pattern[]} */
		const args = [b.id('$$anchor')];
		if (argument) args.push(argument.id);

		const declarations = argument?.declarations ?? [];
		const block = /** @type {BlockStatement} */ (then_context.visit(node.then, then_context.state));

		then_block = b.arrow(args, b.block([...declarations, ...block.body]));
	}

	if (node.catch) {
		const catch_context = { ...context, state: { ...context.state } };
		const argument = node.error && create_derived_block_argument(node.error, catch_context);

		/** @type {Pattern[]} */
		const args = [b.id('$$anchor')];
		if (argument) args.push(argument.id);

		const declarations = argument?.declarations ?? [];
		const block = /** @type {BlockStatement} */ (
			catch_context.visit(node.catch, catch_context.state)
		);

		catch_block = b.arrow(args, b.block([...declarations, ...block.body]));
	}

	context.state.init.push(
		add_svelte_meta(
			b.call(
				'$.await',
				context.state.node,
				expression,
				node.pending
					? b.arrow([b.id('$$anchor')], /** @type {BlockStatement} */ (context.visit(node.pending)))
					: b.null,
				then_block,
				catch_block
			),
			node,
			'await'
		)
	);
}

/**
 * @param {Pattern} node
 * @param {import('zimmerframe').Context<AST.SvelteNode, ComponentClientTransformState>} context
 * @returns {{ id: Pattern, declarations: null | Statement[] }}
 */
function create_derived_block_argument(node, context) {
	if (node.type === 'Identifier') {
		context.state.transform[node.name] = { read: get_value };
		return { id: node, declarations: null };
	}

	const pattern = /** @type {Pattern} */ (context.visit(node));
	const identifiers = extract_identifiers(node);

	const id = b.id('$$source');
	const value = b.id('$$value');

	const block = b.block([
		b.var(pattern, b.call('$.get', id)),
		b.return(b.object(identifiers.map((identifier) => b.prop('init', identifier, identifier))))
	]);

	const declarations = [b.var(value, create_derived(context.state, block))];

	for (const id of identifiers) {
		context.state.transform[id.name] = { read: get_value };

		declarations.push(
			b.var(id, create_derived(context.state, b.member(b.call('$.get', value), id)))
		);
	}

	return { id, declarations };
}

/** @import { Expression, Statement } from 'estree' */
/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../types' */
import { unwrap_optional } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
import { add_svelte_meta, build_expression, Memoizer } from './shared/utils.js';

/**
 * @param {AST.RenderTag} node
 * @param {ComponentContext} context
 */
export function RenderTag(node, context) {
	context.state.template.push_comment();

	const call = unwrap_optional(node.expression);

	/** @type {Expression[]} */
	let args = [];

	const memoizer = new Memoizer();

	for (let i = 0; i < call.arguments.length; i++) {
		const arg = /** @type {Expression} */ (call.arguments[i]);
		const metadata = node.metadata.arguments[i];

		let expression = build_expression(context, arg, metadata);

		if (metadata.has_await || metadata.has_call) {
			expression = b.call('$.get', memoizer.add(expression, metadata.has_await));
		}

		args.push(b.thunk(expression));
	}

	memoizer.apply();

	/** @type {Statement[]} */
	const statements = memoizer.deriveds(context.state.analysis.runes);

	let snippet_function = build_expression(
		context,
		/** @type {Expression} */ (call.callee),
		node.metadata.expression
	);

	if (node.metadata.dynamic) {
		// If we have a chain expression then ensure a nullish snippet function gets turned into an empty one
		if (node.expression.type === 'ChainExpression') {
			snippet_function = b.logical('??', snippet_function, b.id('$.noop'));
		}

		statements.push(
			add_svelte_meta(
				b.call('$.snippet', context.state.node, b.thunk(snippet_function), ...args),
				node,
				'render'
			)
		);
	} else {
		statements.push(
			add_svelte_meta(
				(node.expression.type === 'CallExpression' ? b.call : b.maybe_call)(
					snippet_function,
					context.state.node,
					...args
				),
				node,
				'render'
			)
		);
	}

	const async_values = memoizer.async_values();

	if (async_values) {
		context.state.init.push(
			b.stmt(
				b.call(
					'$.async',
					context.state.node,
					memoizer.async_values(),
					b.arrow([context.state.node, ...memoizer.async_ids()], b.block(statements))
				)
			)
		);
	} else {
		context.state.init.push(statements.length === 1 ? statements[0] : b.block(statements));
	}
}

     3	/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../types' */

     9	/**
    10	 * @param {AST.SnippetBlock} node
    11	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    12	 */
    13	export function SnippetBlock(node, context) {
    14	        // TODO hoist where possible
    15	        /** @type {(Identifier | AssignmentPattern)[]} */
    16	        const args = [b.id('$$anchor')];
    17	        const has_await = node.body.metadata.has_await || false;
    18	
    19	        /** @type {BlockStatement} */
    20	        let body;
    21	
    22	        /** @type {Statement[]} */
    23	        const declarations = [];
    24	
    25	        const transform = { ...context.state.transform };
    26	        const child_state = { ...context.state, transform };
    27	
    28	        for (let i = 0; i < node.parameters.length; i++) {
    29	                const argument = node.parameters[i];
    30	
    31	                if (!argument) continue;
    32	
    33	                if (argument.type === 'Identifier') {
    34	                        args.push(b.assignment_pattern(argument, b.id('$.noop')));
    35	                        transform[argument.name] = { read: b.call };
    36	
    37	                        continue;
    38	                }

    41	                args.push(b.id(arg_alias));

    44

    46	                        id.name = context.state.scope.generate('$$array');
    47	                        transform[id.name] = { read: get_value };

    51	                        );

    53

    55	                        const name = /** @type {Identifier} */ (path.node).name;
    56	                        const needs_derived = path.has_default_value; // to ensure that default value is only called once
    57	                        const fn = b.thunk(/** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(path.expression, child_state)));
    58

    63	                        };

    66	                        // 'Cannot access x before initialization' errors
    67	                        if (dev) {

    78	
    79	        // in dev we use a FunctionExpression (not arrow function) so we can use `arguments`
    80	        let snippet = dev
    81	                ? b.call(
    82	                                '$.wrap_snippet',
    83	                                b.id(context.state.analysis.name),
    84	                                b.function(null, args, body, has_await)
    85	                        )
    86	                : b.arrow(args, body, has_await);
    87	
    88	        const declaration = b.const(node.expression, snippet);
    89	
    90	        // Top-level snippets are hoisted so they can be referenced in the `<script>`
    91	        if (context.path.length === 1 && context.path[0].type === 'Fragment') {
    92	                if (node.metadata.can_hoist) {
    93	                        context.state.module_level_snippets.push(declaration);
    94	                } else {
    95	                        context.state.instance_level_snippets.push(declaration);
    96	                }
    97	        } else {
    98	                context.state.init.push(declaration);
    99	        }
   100	}
   101

/** @import { AST, Binding } from '#compiler' */
/** @import { Scope } from '../../scope' */
/** @import { Context } from '../types' */
import { validate_block_not_empty, validate_opening_tag } from './shared/utils.js';
import * as e from '../../../errors.js';

/**
 * @param {AST.SnippetBlock} node
 * @param {Context} context
 */
export function SnippetBlock(node, context) {
	context.state.analysis.snippets.add(node);

	validate_block_not_empty(node.body, context);

	if (context.state.analysis.runes) {
		validate_opening_tag(node, context.state, '#');
	}

	for (const arg of node.parameters) {
		if (arg.type === 'RestElement') {
			e.snippet_invalid_rest_parameter(arg);
		}
	}

	context.next({ ...context.state, parent_element: null });

	const can_hoist =
		context.path.length === 1 &&
		context.path[0].type === 'Fragment' &&
		can_hoist_snippet(context.state.scope, context.state.scopes);

	const name = node.expression.name;

	if (can_hoist) {
		const binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (context.state.scope.get(name));
		context.state.analysis.module.scope.declarations.set(name, binding);
	}

	node.metadata.can_hoist = can_hoist;

	const { path } = context;
	const parent = path.at(-2);
	if (!parent) return;

	if (
		parent.type === 'Component' &&
		parent.attributes.some(
			(attribute) =>
				(attribute.type === 'Attribute' || attribute.type === 'BindDirective') &&
				attribute.name === node.expression.name
		)
	) {
		e.snippet_shadowing_prop(node, node.expression.name);
	}

	if (node.expression.name !== 'children') return;

	if (
		parent.type === 'Component' ||
		parent.type === 'SvelteComponent' ||
		parent.type === 'SvelteSelf'
	) {
		if (
			parent.fragment.nodes.some(
				(node) =>
					node.type !== 'SnippetBlock' &&
					(node.type !== 'Text' || node.data.trim()) &&
					node.type !== 'Comment'
			)
		) {
			e.snippet_conflict(node);
		}
	}
}

/**
 * @param {Map<AST.SvelteNode, Scope>} scopes
 * @param {Scope} scope
 */
function can_hoist_snippet(scope, scopes, visited = new Set()) {
	for (const [reference] of scope.references) {
		const binding = scope.get(reference);

		if (!binding || binding.scope.function_depth === 0) {
			continue;
		}

		// ignore bindings declared inside the snippet (e.g. the snippet's own parameters)
		if (binding.scope.function_depth >= scope.function_depth) {
			continue;
		}

		if (binding.initial?.type === 'SnippetBlock') {
			if (visited.has(binding)) continue;
			visited.add(binding);
			const snippet_scope = /** @type {Scope} */ (scopes.get(binding.initial));

			if (can_hoist_snippet(snippet_scope, scopes, visited)) {
				continue;
			}
		}

		return false;
	}

	return true;
}

import type { Scope } from '../scope.js';
import type { ComponentAnalysis, ReactiveStatement } from '../types.js';
import type { AST, ExpressionMetadata, StateField, ValidatedCompileOptions } from '#compiler';

export interface AnalysisState {
	scope: Scope;
	scopes: Map<AST.SvelteNode, Scope>;
	analysis: ComponentAnalysis;
	options: ValidatedCompileOptions;
	ast_type: 'instance' | 'template' | 'module';
	fragment: AST.Fragment | null;
	/**
	 * Tag name of the parent element. `null` if the parent is `svelte:element`, `#snippet`, a component or the root.
	 * Parent doesn't necessarily mean direct path predecessor because there could be `#each`, `#if` etc in-between.
	 */
	parent_element: string | null;
	has_props_rune: boolean;
	/** Which slots the current parent component has */
	component_slots: Set<string>;
	/** Information about the current expression/directive/block value */
	expression: ExpressionMetadata | null;

	/** Used to analyze class state */
	state_fields: Map<string, StateField>;

	function_depth: number;

	// legacy stuff
	reactive_statement: null | ReactiveStatement;
}

export type Context<State extends AnalysisState = AnalysisState> = import('zimmerframe').Context<
	AST.SvelteNode,
	State
>;

export type Visitors<State extends AnalysisState = AnalysisState> = import('zimmerframe').Visitors<
	AST.SvelteNode,
	State
>;

 * @param {AST.SnippetBlock} node
 * @param {ComponentContext} context
 */
export function SnippetBlock(node, context) {
	// TODO hoist where possible
	/** @type {(Identifier | AssignmentPattern)[]} */
	const args = [b.id('$$anchor')];
	const has_await = node.body.metadata.has_await || false;

	// Snippets compile to standalone functions. If they reference identifiers that
	// only exist in an outer scope (e.g. the `then`/`catch` value of an {#await} block),
	// those identifiers must be passed to the snippet function.
	/** @type {AST.Identifier[]} */
	const captures = node.metadata?.captures ?? [];
	/** @type {Map<string, string>} */
	const capture_aliases = new Map();
	for (let i = 0; i < captures.length; i++) {
		const name = captures[i].name;
		const alias = `$$capture${i}`;
		capture_aliases.set(name, alias);
		args.push(b.id(alias));
	}

	/** @type {BlockStatement} */
	let body;

	/** @type {Statement[]} */
	const declarations = [];

	const transform = { ...context.state.transform };
	// Ensure references inside the snippet body read from the captured arguments
	for (const [name, alias] of capture_aliases) {
		transform[name] = { read: () => b.id(alias) };
	}
	const child_state = { ...context.state, transform };

	for (let i = 0; i < node.parameters.length; i++) {
		const argument = node.parameters[i];

		if (!argument) continue;

		if (argument.type === 'Identifier') {
			args.push(b.assignment_pattern(argument, b.id('$.noop')));
			transform[argument.name] = { read: b.call };

			continue;
		}

		let arg_alias = `$$arg${i}`;
		args.push(b.id(arg_alias));

/** @import { AST, Binding } from '#compiler' */
/** @import { Scope } from '../../scope' */
/** @import { Context } from '../types' */
import { validate_block_not_empty, validate_opening_tag } from './shared/utils.js';
import * as e from '../../../errors.js';

/**
 * @param {AST.SnippetBlock} node
 * @param {Context} context
 */
export function SnippetBlock(node, context) {
	context.state.analysis.snippets.add(node);

	validate_block_not_empty(node.body, context);

	if (context.state.analysis.runes) {
		validate_opening_tag(node, context.state, '#');
	}

	for (const arg of node.parameters) {
		if (arg.type === 'RestElement') {
			e.snippet_invalid_rest_parameter(arg);
		}
	}

	context.next({ ...context.state, parent_element: null });

	const can_hoist =
		context.path.length === 1 &&
		context.path[0].type === 'Fragment' &&
		can_hoist_snippet(context.state.scope, context.state.scopes);

	const name = node.expression.name;

	if (can_hoist) {
		const binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (context.state.scope.get(name));
		context.state.analysis.module.scope.declarations.set(name, binding);
	}

	node.metadata.can_hoist = can_hoist;

	// In `experimental.async` mode, snippets are invoked like functions and do not
	// automatically close over variables from surrounding template scopes (e.g.
	// {#await ... then value}). Record which identifiers the snippet references so
	// the transform phase can pass them in.
	if (context.state.options.experimental.async) {
		/** @type {AST.Identifier[]} */
		const captures = [];
		for (const [reference] of context.state.scope.references) {
			const binding = context.state.scope.get(reference);
			if (!binding) continue;
			// capture variables declared outside of the snippet itself
			if (binding.scope.function_depth < context.state.scope.function_depth) {
				captures.push(/** @type {AST.Identifier} */ ({ type: 'Identifier', name: reference }));
			}
		}
		node.metadata.captures = captures;
	}

	const { path } = context;
	const parent = path.at(-2);
	if (!parent) return;

	if (
		parent.type === 'Component' &&
		parent.attributes.some(
			(attribute) =>
				(attribute.type === 'Attribute' || attribute.type === 'BindDirective') &&
				attribute.name === node.expression.name
		)
	) {
		e.snippet_shadowing_prop(node, node.expression.name);
	}

	if (node.expression.name !== 'children') return;

	if (
		parent.type === 'Component' ||
		parent.type === 'SvelteComponent' ||
		parent.type === 'SvelteSelf'
	) {
		if (
			parent.fragment.nodes.some(
				(node) =>
					node.type !== 'SnippetBlock' &&
					(node.type !== 'Text' || node.data.trim()) &&
					node.type !== 'Comment'
			)
		) {
			e.snippet_conflict(node);

from pathlib import Path
path=Path('/testbed/packages/svelte/src/compiler/phases/3-transform/client/visitors/RenderTag.js')
text=path.read_text()
marker="\tmemoizer.apply();\n"
if marker not in text:
    raise SystemExit('marker not found')
insert="""\n\t// If this renders a statically-known snippet, pass through any implicitly\n\t// captured identifiers so the snippet can reference outer-scope values\n\t// (e.g. the `then`/`catch` value of an {#await} block) without declaring them\n\t// as snippet parameters.
\tif (call.callee.type === 'Identifier') {
\t\tconst binding = context.state.scope.get(call.callee.name);
\t\tif (binding?.initial?.type === 'SnippetBlock') {
\t\t\tconst captures = binding.initial.metadata?.captures ?? [];
\t\t\tfor (const capture of captures) {
\t\t\t\targs.push(b.thunk(/** @type {any} */ (context.visit(capture))));
\t\t\t}
\t\t}
\t}
\n"""
text=text.replace(marker, insert+marker)
path.write_text(text)
print('updated')

/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
/** @import { Context } from '../types' */
import { unwrap_optional } from '../../../utils/ast.js';
import * as e from '../../../errors.js';
import { validate_opening_tag } from './shared/utils.js';
import { mark_subtree_dynamic } from './shared/fragment.js';
import { is_resolved_snippet } from './shared/snippets.js';
import { create_expression_metadata } from '../../nodes.js';

/**
 * @param {AST.RenderTag} node
 * @param {Context} context
 */
export function RenderTag(node, context) {
	validate_opening_tag(node, context.state, '@');

	node.metadata.path = [...context.path];

	const expression = unwrap_optional(node.expression);
	const callee = expression.callee;

	const binding = callee.type === 'Identifier' ? context.state.scope.get(callee.name) : null;
	node.metadata.binding = binding;

	node.metadata.dynamic = binding?.kind !== 'normal';

	/**
	 * If we can't unambiguously resolve this to a declaration, we
	 * must assume the worst and link the render tag to every snippet
	 */
	let resolved = callee.type === 'Identifier' && is_resolved_snippet(binding);

	if (binding?.initial?.type === 'SnippetBlock') {
		// if this render tag unambiguously references a local snippet, our job is easy
		node.metadata.snippets.add(binding.initial);
	}

	context.state.analysis.snippet_renderers.set(node, resolved);
	context.state.analysis.uses_render_tags = true;

	const raw_args = unwrap_optional(node.expression).arguments;
	for (const arg of raw_args) {
		if (arg.type === 'SpreadElement') {
			e.render_tag_invalid_spread_argument(arg);
		}
	}

	if (
		callee.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
		callee.property.type === 'Identifier' &&
		['bind', 'apply', 'call'].includes(callee.property.name)
	) {
		e.render_tag_invalid_call_expression(node);
	}

	mark_subtree_dynamic(context.path);

	context.visit(callee, { ...context.state, expression: node.metadata.expression });

	for (const arg of expression.arguments) {
		const metadata = create_expression_metadata();
		node.metadata.arguments.push(metadata);

		context.visit(arg, {
			...context.state,
			expression: metadata
		});
	}
}

from pathlib import Path
path=Path('/testbed/packages/svelte/src/compiler/phases/2-analyze/visitors/SnippetBlock.js')
text=path.read_text().splitlines(True)
# after context.next(...) line insert capture calc in correct scope
out=[]
inserted=False
for line in text:
    out.append(line)
    if not inserted and line.strip().startswith('context.next('):
        out.append("\n\t// Determine which outer-scope identifiers this snippet references (async mode only).\n")
        out.append("\t// Needs to happen after visiting the snippet body so that scope.references is complete.\n")
        out.append("\tif (context.state.options.experimental.async) {\n")
        out.append("\t\t/** @type {AST.Identifier[]} */\n")
        out.append("\t\tconst captures = [];\n")
        out.append("\t\tfor (const [reference] of context.state.scope.references) {\n")
        out.append("\t\t\tconst binding = context.state.scope.get(reference);\n")
        out.append("\t\t\tif (!binding) continue;\n")
        out.append("\t\t\tif (binding.scope.function_depth < context.state.scope.function_depth) {\n")
        out.append("\t\t\t\tcaptures.push(/** @type {AST.Identifier} */ ({ type: 'Identifier', name: reference }));\n")
        out.append("\t\t\t}\n")
        out.append("\t\t}\n")
        out.append("\t\tnode.metadata.captures = captures;\n")
        out.append("\t}\n")
        inserted=True
# remove earlier block we inserted after can_hoist
joined=''.join(out)
start=joined.find("\n\t// In `experimental.async` mode")
if start!=-1:
    end=joined.find("\n\tconst { path }", start)
    joined = joined[:start] + "\n" + joined[end:]
path.write_text(joined)
print('updated')

/** @import { AST, Binding } from '#compiler' */
/** @import { Scope } from '../../scope' */
/** @import { Context } from '../types' */
import { validate_block_not_empty, validate_opening_tag } from './shared/utils.js';
import * as e from '../../../errors.js';

/**
 * @param {AST.SnippetBlock} node
 * @param {Context} context
 */
export function SnippetBlock(node, context) {
	context.state.analysis.snippets.add(node);

	validate_block_not_empty(node.body, context);

	if (context.state.analysis.runes) {
		validate_opening_tag(node, context.state, '#');
	}

	for (const arg of node.parameters) {
		if (arg.type === 'RestElement') {
			e.snippet_invalid_rest_parameter(arg);
		}
	}

	context.next({ ...context.state, parent_element: null });

	// Determine which outer-scope identifiers this snippet references (async mode only).
	// Needs to happen after visiting the snippet body so that scope.references is complete.
	if (context.state.options.experimental.async) {
		/** @type {AST.Identifier[]} */
		const captures = [];
		for (const [reference] of context.state.scope.references) {
			const binding = context.state.scope.get(reference);
			if (!binding) continue;
			if (binding.scope.function_depth < context.state.scope.function_depth) {
				captures.push(/** @type {AST.Identifier} */ ({ type: 'Identifier', name: reference }));
			}
		}
		node.metadata.captures = captures;
	}

	const can_hoist =
		context.path.length === 1 &&
		context.path[0].type === 'Fragment' &&
		can_hoist_snippet(context.state.scope, context.state.scopes);

	const name = node.expression.name;

	if (can_hoist) {
		const binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (context.state.scope.get(name));
		context.state.analysis.module.scope.declarations.set(name, binding);
	}

	node.metadata.can_hoist = can_hoist;


	const { path } = context;
	const parent = path.at(-2);
	if (!parent) return;

	if (
		parent.type === 'Component' &&
		parent.attributes.some(
			(attribute) =>
				(attribute.type === 'Attribute' || attribute.type === 'BindDirective') &&
				attribute.name === node.expression.name
		)
	) {
		e.snippet_shadowing_prop(node, node.expression.name);

path=Path('/testbed/packages/svelte/src/compiler/phases/2-analyze/visitors/SnippetBlock.js')
text=path.read_text()
# move capture block to after can_hoist assignment
import re
m=re.search(r"\n\t// Determine which outer-scope identifiers[\s\S]*?\tnode\.metadata\.captures = captures;\n\t}\n", text)
if not m:
    raise SystemExit('capture block not found')
cap=m.group(0)

/** @import { AST, Binding } from '#compiler' */
/** @import { Scope } from '../../scope' */
/** @import { Context } from '../types' */
import { validate_block_not_empty, validate_opening_tag } from './shared/utils.js';
import * as e from '../../../errors.js';

/**
 * @param {AST.SnippetBlock} node
 * @param {Context} context
 */
export function SnippetBlock(node, context) {
	context.state.analysis.snippets.add(node);

	validate_block_not_empty(node.body, context);

	if (context.state.analysis.runes) {
		validate_opening_tag(node, context.state, '#');
	}

	for (const arg of node.parameters) {
		if (arg.type === 'RestElement') {
			e.snippet_invalid_rest_parameter(arg);
		}
	}

	context.next({ ...context.state, parent_element: null });


	const can_hoist =
		context.path.length === 1 &&
		context.path[0].type === 'Fragment' &&
		can_hoist_snippet(context.state.scope, context.state.scopes);

	const name = node.expression.name;

	if (can_hoist) {
		const binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (context.state.scope.get(name));
		context.state.analysis.module.scope.declarations.set(name, binding);
	}

	node.metadata.can_hoist = can_hoist;

	// Determine which outer-scope identifiers this snippet references (async mode only).
	// Needs to happen after visiting the snippet body so that scope.references is complete.
	if (context.state.options.experimental.async) {
		/** @type {AST.Identifier[]} */
		const captures = [];
		const snippet_scope = /** @type {Scope} */ (context.state.scopes.get(node));
		for (const [reference] of snippet_scope.references) {
			const binding = snippet_scope.get(reference);
			if (!binding) continue;
			if (binding.scope.function_depth < snippet_scope.function_depth) {
				captures.push(/** @type {AST.Identifier} */ ({ type: 'Identifier', name: reference }));
			}
		}
		node.metadata.captures = captures;
	}


	const { path } = context;
	const parent = path.at(-2);
	if (!parent) return;

	if (
		parent.type === 'Component' &&
		parent.attributes.some(
			(attribute) =>
				(attribute.type === 'Attribute' || attribute.type === 'BindDirective') &&
				attribute.name === node.expression.name
		)
	) {
		e.snippet_shadowing_prop(node, node.expression.name);
	}

	if (node.expression.name !== 'children') return;

	if (
		parent.type === 'Component' ||
		parent.type === 'SvelteComponent' ||
		parent.type === 'SvelteSelf'

from pathlib import Path
path=Path('/testbed/packages/svelte/src/compiler/phases/2-analyze/visitors/SnippetBlock.js')
text=path.read_text().splitlines(True)
# insert before context.next line

import subprocess, textwrap
js=textwrap.dedent('''
const svelte = require('./packages/svelte/compiler');
const src = `
<script>
  async function get() { return 1; }
  const promise = get();
</script>
{#await promise then value}
  {#snippet s()}{value}{/snippet}
  {@render s()}
{/await}
`;
const out = svelte.compile(src,{filename:'Test.svelte',generate:'client',dev:true,experimental:{async:true}});
function find(node, type){
 if(!node) return null;
 if(node.type===type) return node;
 for(const k in node){
  const v=node[k];
  if(Array.isArray(v)){
    for(const c of v){ if(c && typeof c==='object'){ const r=find(c,type); if(r) return r; } }
  } else if(v && typeof v==='object'){
    const r=find(v,type); if(r) return r;
  }
 }
 return null;
}
const snip=find(out.ast.html,'SnippetBlock');
console.log('captures', snip.metadata && snip.metadata.captures);
''')

import subprocess, textwrap
js=textwrap.dedent('''
const svelte = require('./packages/svelte/compiler');
const src = `
<script>
  async function get() { return 1; }
  const promise = get();
</script>
{#await promise then value}
  {#snippet s()}{value}{/snippet}
  {@render s()}
{/await}
`;
const out = svelte.compile(src,{filename:'Test.svelte',generate:'client',dev:true,experimental:{async:true}});
function find(node, type){
 if(!node) return null;
 if(node.type===type) return node;
 for(const k in node){
  const v=node[k];
  if(Array.isArray(v)){
    for(const c of v){ if(c && typeof c==='object'){ const r=find(c,type); if(r) return r; } }
  } else if(v && typeof v==='object'){
    const r=find(v,type); if(r) return r;
  }
 }
 return null;
}
const snip=find(out.ast.html,'SnippetBlock');
console.log('body captures', snip.body && snip.body.metadata && snip.body.metadata.captures);
''')
res=subprocess.run(['node','-e',js],cwd='/testbed',capture_output=True,text=True)
print(res.stderr)
print(res.stdout)

import { JSDOM } from 'jsdom';
import vm from 'node:vm';
import { compile } from './packages/svelte/compiler/index.js';

const src = `
<script>
  async function get() { return 1; }
  const promise = get();
</script>
{#await promise then value}
  {#snippet s()}{value}{/snippet}
  {@render s()}
{/await}
`;

const out = compile(src,{filename:'Test.svelte',generate:'client',dev:false,experimental:{async:true}});

const dom = new JSDOM('<!doctype html><div id="app"></div>',{runScripts:'outside-only'});
const context = { window: dom.window, document: dom.window.document, console, setTimeout, clearTimeout, Promise, Text, Comment, Node: dom.window.Node, Element: dom.window.Element };
context.globalThis = context;

// provide module loader for svelte/internal/client
const modules = new Map();
modules.set('svelte/internal/client', await import('./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/index.js'));
modules.set('svelte/internal/disclose-version', {});
modules.set('svelte/internal/flags/legacy', {});
modules.set('svelte/internal/flags/async', {});

function run(code){
  const wrapped = `(async function(require){ ${code}; return Test; })`;
  const fn = vm.runInNewContext(wrapped, context);
  return fn((id)=>modules.get(id));
}

const Test = await run(out.js.code);
const target = dom.window.document.getElementById('app');
Test(target,{});
await new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,0));
console.log(target.textContent.trim());

+import subprocess, textwrap
+js=textwrap.dedent('''
+const svelte = require('./packages/svelte/compiler');
+const src = `
+<script>
+  async function get() { return 1; }
+  const promise = get();
+</script>
+{#await promise then value}
+  {#snippet s()}{value}{/snippet}
+  {@render s()}
+{/await}
+`;
+const out = svelte.compile(src,{filename:'Test.svelte',generate:'client',dev:true,experimental:{async:true}});
+function find(node, type){
+ if(!node) return null;
+ if(node.type===type) return node;
+ for(const k in node){
+  const v=node[k];
+  if(Array.isArray(v)){
+    for(const c of v){ if(c && typeof c==='object'){ const r=find(c,type); if(r) return r; } }
+  } else if(v && typeof v==='object'){
+    const r=find(v,type); if(r) return r;
+  }
+ }
+ return null;
+}
+const snip=find(out.ast.html,'SnippetBlock');
+console.log('captures', snip.metadata && snip.metadata.captures);
+''')
+res=subprocess.run(['node','-e',js],cwd='/testbed',capture_output=True,text=True)

diff --git a/edit_analyze_snippet.py b/edit_analyze_snippet.py
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..fa5d805a1
--- /dev/null
+++ b/edit_analyze_snippet.py
@@ -0,0 +1,32 @@
+from pathlib import Path
+path=Path('/testbed/packages/svelte/src/compiler/phases/2-analyze/visitors/SnippetBlock.js')
+text=path.read_text().splitlines(True)
+# insert after node.metadata.can_hoist = can_hoist;
+needle='\tnode.metadata.can_hoist = can_hoist;\n'
+out=[]
+inserted=False
+for line in text:
+    out.append(line)
+    if not inserted and line==needle:
+        out.append("\n\t// In `experimental.async` mode, snippets are invoked like functions and do not\n")
+        out.append("\t// automatically close over variables from surrounding template scopes (e.g.\n")
+        out.append("\t// {#await ... then value}). Record which identifiers the snippet references so\n")
+        out.append("\t// the transform phase can pass them in.\n")
+        out.append("\tif (context.state.options.experimental.async) {\n")
+        out.append("\t\t/** @type {AST.Identifier[]} */\n")
+        out.append("\t\tconst captures = [];\n")
+        out.append("\t\tfor (const [reference] of context.state.scope.references) {\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\tconst binding = context.state.scope.get(reference);\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\tif (!binding) continue;\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\t// capture variables declared outside of the snippet itself\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\tif (binding.scope.function_depth < context.state.scope.function_depth) {\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\t\tcaptures.push(/** @type {AST.Identifier} */ ({ type: 'Identifier', name: reference }));\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\t}\n")
+        out.append("\t\t}\n")
+        out.append("\t\tnode.metadata.captures = captures;\n")
+        out.append("\t}\n")
+        inserted=True
+if not inserted:
+    raise SystemExit('insertion point not found')
+path.write_text(''.join(out))
+print('updated')

+from pathlib import Path
+path=Path('/testbed/packages/svelte/src/compiler/phases/3-transform/client/visitors/RenderTag.js')
+text=path.read_text().splitlines(True)
+out=[]
+for line in text:
+    out.append(line)
+    if line.strip()=="let args = [];":
+        # later after args built we will add capture args; easier insert after args loop
+        pass
+# insert after for loop that builds args, before memoizer.apply()
+joined=''.join(out)
+needle="\tfor (let i = 0; i < call.arguments.length; i++) {\n"
+idx=joined.find(needle)
+if idx==-1:
+    raise SystemExit('needle not found')
+# find end of loop by locating "\tmemoizer.apply();"
+end=joined.find("\n\tmemoizer.apply();", idx)
+if end==-1:
+    raise SystemExit('end not found')
+pre=joined[:end]
+post=joined[end:]
+insert="\n\t// If this is a render of a statically-known snippet, pass through any\n\t// implicitly-captured identifiers so the snippet can reference outer-scope values\n\t// (e.g. values introduced by {#await ... then value}).\n\tconst callee_binding = context.state.scope.get(call.callee.type === 'Identifier' ? call.callee.name : null);\n\tif (callee_binding?.initial?.type === 'SnippetBlock') {\n\t\tconst captures = callee_binding.initial.metadata?.captures ?? [];\n\t\tfor (const capture of captures) {\n\t\t\targs.push(b.thunk(build_expression(context, capture, { has_await: false, has_call: false })));\n\t\t}\n\t}\n"
+# build_expression expects metadata, but we don't have. We'll simplify by using capture identifier via context.visit? This might be wrong.

+from pathlib import Path
+path = Path('/testbed/packages/svelte/src/compiler/phases/3-transform/client/visitors/SnippetBlock.js')
+text = path.read_text()
+old = """\t// TODO hoist where possible\n\t/** @type {(Identifier | AssignmentPattern)[]} */\n\tconst args = [b.id('$$anchor')];\n\tconst has_await = node.body.metadata.has_await || false;\n\n\t/** @type {BlockStatement} */\n\tlet body;\n\n\t/** @type {Statement[]} */\n\tconst declarations = [];\n\n\tconst transform = { ...context.state.transform };\n\tconst child_state = { ...context.state, transform };\n"""
+new = """\t// TODO hoist where possible\n\t/** @type {(Identifier | AssignmentPattern)[]} */\n\tconst args = [b.id('$$anchor')];\n\tconst has_await = node.body.metadata.has_await || false;\n\n\t// Snippets compile to standalone functions. If they reference identifiers that\n\t// only exist in an outer scope (e.g. the `then`/`catch` value of an {#await} block),\n\t// those identifiers must be passed to the snippet function.\n\t/** @type {AST.Identifier[]} */\n\tconst captures = node.metadata?.captures ?? [];\n\t/** @type {Map<string, string>} */\n\tconst capture_aliases = new Map();\n\tfor (let i = 0; i < captures.length; i++) {\n\t\tconst name = captures[i].name;\n\t\tconst alias = `$$capture${i}`;\n\t\tcapture_aliases.set(name, alias);\n\t\targs.push(b.id(alias));\n\t}\n\n\t/** @type {BlockStatement} */\n\tlet body;\n\n\t/** @type {Statement[]} */\n\tconst declarations = [];\n\n\tconst transform = { ...context.state.transform };\n\t// Ensure references inside the snippet body read from the captured arguments\n\tfor (const [name, alias] of capture_aliases) {\n\t\ttransform[name] = { read: () => b.id(alias) };\n\t}\n\tconst child_state = { ...context.state, transform };\n"""
+if old not in text:
+    raise SystemExit('old block not found')
+path.write_text(text.replace(old, new))
+print('updated')

+export default function Test($$anchor, $$props) {
+	$.check_target(new.target);
+	$.push($$props, false, Test);
+
+	async function get() {
+		return 1;
+	}
+

+	var fragment = $.comment();
+	var node = $.first_child(fragment);
+

+		() => $.await(node, () => promise, null, ($$anchor, value) => {

+				$.validate_snippet_args(...arguments);
+				$.next();
+
+				var text = $.text();
+
+				$.template_effect(() => $.set_text(text, $.get(value)));
+				$.append($$anchor, text);
+			});

+		}),
+		'await',
+		Test,
+		7,
+		0
+	);

+	$.append($$anchor, fragment);
+
+	return $.pop({ ...$.legacy_api() });

+	/** @type {Map<string, string>} */
+	const capture_aliases = new Map();
+	for (let i = 0; i < captures.length; i++) {
+		const name = captures[i].name;
+		const alias = `$$capture${i}`;
+		capture_aliases.set(name, alias);
+		args.push(b.id(alias));
+	}
+
 	/** @type {BlockStatement} */
 	let body;

+	}

+from pathlib import Path
+path=Path('/testbed/packages/svelte/src/compiler/phases/2-analyze/visitors/SnippetBlock.js')
+text=path.read_text().splitlines(True)
+# after context.next(...) line insert capture calc in correct scope
+out=[]
+inserted=False
+for line in text:
+    out.append(line)
+    if not inserted and line.strip().startswith('context.next('):
+        out.append("\n\t// Determine which outer-scope identifiers this snippet references (async mode only).\n")
+        out.append("\t// Needs to happen after visiting the snippet body so that scope.references is complete.\n")
+        out.append("\tif (context.state.options.experimental.async) {\n")
+        out.append("\t\t/** @type {AST.Identifier[]} */\n")
+        out.append("\t\tconst captures = [];\n")
+        out.append("\t\tfor (const [reference] of context.state.scope.references) {\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\tconst binding = context.state.scope.get(reference);\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\tif (!binding) continue;\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\tif (binding.scope.function_depth < context.state.scope.function_depth) {\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\t\tcaptures.push(/** @type {AST.Identifier} */ ({ type: 'Identifier', name: reference }));\n")
+        out.append("\t\t\t}\n")
+        out.append("\t\t}\n")
+        out.append("\t\tnode.metadata.captures = captures;\n")
+        out.append("\t}\n")
+        inserted=True
+# remove earlier block we inserted after can_hoist
+joined=''.join(out)
+start=joined.find("\n\t// In `experimental.async` mode")
+if start!=-1:
+    end=joined.find("\n\tconst { path }", start)
+    joined = joined[:start] + "\n" + joined[end:]
+path.write_text(joined)
+print('updated')

+import subprocess, textwrap, json, os, sys, tempfile, pathlib
+
+def compile_svelte(source: str, *, experimental_async=True):
+    node = textwrap.dedent(f"""
+    const svelte = require('./packages/svelte/compiler');
+    const src = {json.dumps(source)};
+    const out = svelte.compile(src, {{
+      filename: 'Test.svelte',
+      generate: 'client',
+      dev: true,
+      experimental: {{ async: {str(experimental_async).lower()} }},
+    }});
+    console.log(out.js.code);
+    """)
+    res = subprocess.run(['node','-e',node], cwd='/testbed', capture_output=True, text=True)
+    if res.returncode!=0:
+        print(res.stderr)
+        raise SystemExit(res.returncode)
+    return res.stdout
+
+src = r"""
+<script>
+  async function get() { return 1; }
+  const promise = get();
+</script>
+
+{#await promise then value}
+  {#snippet s()}
+    {value}
+  {/snippet}
+  {@render s()}
+{/await}
+"""
+print(compile_svelte(src))

+import { JSDOM } from 'jsdom';
+import vm from 'node:vm';
+import { compile } from './packages/svelte/compiler/index.js';
+
+const src = `
+<script>
+  async function get() { return 1; }
+  const promise = get();
+</script>
+{#await promise then value}
+  {#snippet s()}{value}{/snippet}
+  {@render s()}
+{/await}
+`;
+
+const out = compile(src,{filename:'Test.svelte',generate:'client',dev:false,experimental:{async:true}});
+
+const dom = new JSDOM('<!doctype html><div id="app"></div>',{runScripts:'outside-only'});
+const context = { window: dom.window, document: dom.window.document, console, setTimeout, clearTimeout, Promise, Text, Comment, Node: dom.window.Node, Element: dom.window.Element };
+context.globalThis = context;
+
+// provide module loader for svelte/internal/client
+const modules = new Map();
+modules.set('svelte/internal/client', await import('./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/index.js'));
+modules.set('svelte/internal/disclose-version', {});
+modules.set('svelte/internal/flags/legacy', {});
+modules.set('svelte/internal/flags/async', {});
+
+function run(code){
+  const wrapped = `(async function(require){ ${code}; return Test; })`;
+  const fn = vm.runInNewContext(wrapped, context);
+  return fn((id)=>modules.get(id));
+}
+
+const Test = await run(out.js.code);
+const target = dom.window.document.getElementById('app');
+Test(target,{});
+await new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,0));
+console.log(target.textContent.trim());
